puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	 then place them one on top of the other in the shape of a cross, and tie the sinus, which we have said is below the skin of the knees, with a strong ligature made of two parts.
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	 then wrap the threads with more threads and tie them firmly with two parts, so that no foreign body can enter, lest an abscess form there.
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	 and place the ligature again according to the first one, two finger-widths from that one, and after these two ligatures leave the sinus which is below the skin of the knees open to the size of a finger.
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	 And then all the others according to the roundness of the egg.
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	 Then cut in the part that is under the skin of the knees, so that the blood flows and swells, as we have said before.
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	 Then apply wool soaked in oil to the wounds, and apply the bandage that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	 And sometimes the white flesh is cauterized after the incision, out of fear of bleeding.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	 For this happens often, and leave the bandage until it falls off on its own.
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	 And if it is slow to fall off, then it should be softened with hot water, and apply what we have said until it falls off.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 Then treat the wound with another treatment until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	 of fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	 In this manner, I have never seen anyone who dared to perform the treatment with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	 And the ancients said that it is done like the cord that is with the bolt, in such a way that you tie the vessels lightly from below after cutting.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	 then chop inside, and treat the abscess of whoever works, until the patient faints.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and treat it as we have said, until he is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	 Sometimes the infection reaches the veins, as we have said, and opens up the place.
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	 and none of the intestines should be cut as the kidneys, and if any are cut, it is bad, and they come back every hour.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	 however, if it lingers too long in this spot, the wound or ulcer swells until the intestines are cut.
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	 and this happens due to the swelling of the ulcer which is in the veins, as we have said, because it expands, then the place becomes softened and inflamed and open. abei
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	 And the treatment is by cautery, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	 And sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	 and let the patient lie on their back between your hands, then cut the swollen place wide according to the quantity of three fingers;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	 and then remove the pus that is under the skin with a needle, then take a bandage and place it on the visible part of the pus; ️
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	 and press firmly on the belly, then stitch together the two visible parts of the pus at the top of the bandage, and sew one to the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	 then remove the head of the bandage, and do not cut or spread the pus or anything else, as I have told you in the treatment of the intestinal hernia;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	 Then treat by treating the wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 And when you cut the threads, cleanse and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	 The syphilitic person is confined, and there is no appearance of scabs, and the cautery is moved to this place, and it is closer to salvation.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	 of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	 Often the skin of the testicles is softened in some men, because the contents within are softened, and it can be seen like milk;
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	 And it is necessary that when one wants to treat it, the patient lies on his back and cuts off the softened skin onto the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	 then join the two lips with one stitch, and if you wish, first suture the excess of the softened skin at three or four points firmly.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	 Then cut between the stitches, and treat as with other wounds until it heals, and let the threads fall off.
dou chastrement	 Of the castration
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	 Know that castration is abominable in our law, and therefore it pleases me not to speak of it in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	 et il n’est nécessaire de faire cela que pour deux raisons :
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	 the other is that the physician knows how to answer when asked and knows how to perform the cure;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	 and the other reason is that we often need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as goats, sheep, and others.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	 Therefore, I say that castration is done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	 either by attraction or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	 In the method we use by attraction, we make the animal sit in hot water until the testicles are softened and hanging;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	 then take them in your hand until they are removed and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	 About the castration of the tail:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	 It is necessary that you dye the animal, and press its skin with your left hand, then tie the suspension, and cut over each ear once, when you have well flayed them.
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	 And leave some of the subtle fat that is on the vessels.
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	 And this method of castration is better than that done by attraction, because in attraction there may remain something of the skin, which causes the animal to desire lust.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 Then heal the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	 Of hermaphrodites:
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	 Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways in men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	 One way is that between the two testicles there appears as if by nature the figure of a woman, with hair, and sometimes it excretes urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	 And the other manner is in women, and it extends from the wrist like a rod and two fingers.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	 And the treatment for a man and a woman is that you cut off all the flesh close by, and treat it as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	 in the second manner, of men whose urine passes through the skin of the scrotum, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	 Of the swelling
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	 Tentigen is flesh attached to the natural part, as long as it is too unsightly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	 and some women have it as large as a hand, and this is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	 It is necessary that you dye the excess of the tentigen in your hand or with tweezers, and cut it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 and do not go too deep, so that bleeding does not occur, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	 And at another place which is born at the mouth of the womb, and it fills up, and perhaps it jumps forth, and it resembles a cow, and therefore the ancients called it "cow disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 If it becomes necessary for you to cut it, as we have said about the tendon, then continue the treatment until it is healed.
de erratique	 of error
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	 It is erratic when the woman's nature is not perceived, or the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	 and it is either natural from birth, or accidental due to a disease that has come upon her.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	 Or it is caused by a nearby growth, or by a subtle or thick secretion, and it is formed deep in the womb, or on the side, or below, wherever it may be.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	 and it prevents conception, and childbirth, and perhaps even menstruation.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	 And knowledge of this is by looking at the valley.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	 If the swelling appears near, seek for yourself two or three [remedies].
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	 If it is a subtle syphon, and it is close to two pounds, then hurry, and let it run thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	 put your two fingers together, and the woman should be on her back, with her legs spread;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	 then let there be the two pounds strongly, so that the subtle syphon runs well, and beware of blocking;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	 then take wool, wet it with oil, and put it on the place, and let the woman lie down every day, so that it cannot heal.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	 And if the suture is hard and thick, then you must cut it with a spatula resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	 If the blockage is of natural flesh, then suspend it with a hook and cut it.
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	 and have the medicines that stop bleeding, such as vinegar, dragon's blood, incense, mixed with plenty of egg; xspace
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	 then bring a wide lead plate, so that the wound cannot heal;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	 and thus it should be for a long time, and bring him a tent of dry linen;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then he should be treated with other treatments until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	 And when in the flesh comes a tumor, it should be cut according to this manner, unless it is an infected abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	 For an infected abscess that is in the flesh, one should not attempt to cut.
des emorroides	 of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	 Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that usually have no skin, and when hemorrhoids are old, they become hard;
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	 and we have already said in the division their similarities, and the signs, and I will say here those which receive treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	 I say that hemorrhoids and thinning, when they are deeply embedded in the flesh and do not appear to touch, then the cure is not by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	 Those who are at the edge of death, which one can sense, are those whom one can cure.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	 Therefore, you should put the woman in a cold house, then stretch the hard thing with tongs, and cut it at its roots, then sprinkle on powders that restrict blood flow, such as vinegar, dragon's blood, and incense, and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	 Then put his feet against the wall for an hour, then place him in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	 And if bleeding follows, then have her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate bark and galls and similar things; then take barley flour and mix it with honey and vinegar, and make one plaster on his back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	 And if he faints, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	 If not, apply cupping glasses to the back and breasts without pricking.
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	 Then take linen, wet it in plantain juice or hawthorn juice with old wine, and apply to the place.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And when the abscess has subsided, treat the place with onion ointment until it is healed.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	 And that which is called “albathir” is red, and it resembles a sharp chief, so you must cover it as I have said about the tel.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then let the wound heal completely.
des apostemes de la marris	 of the abscesses of the buttocks
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	 Many kinds of abscesses come in the buttocks, such as chancres and pious abscesses and herpes and ulcers and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscess, and many other illnesses that I have spoken of in the section on classification.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	 It is therefore necessary that I speak in this treatise about the hot abscess which comes from the marrow, which is not one of the abscesses that swell up.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	 And if you wish to know the work of iron, look to see if the abscess is sharp at its beginning and full of heat and fever, and if it turns red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	 Then do not hurry to pierce, but let the abscess mature until the pain is soothed;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	 And then make the patient sit on the chair, and have two small chairs where he leans back, and place it on his back, and bring his feet together outside the leg.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	 And let his thighs be spread apart, and place his arms under his knees, and tie them well with a good rope.
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	 Then the cup is placed towards the right side, and the instrument with which one works the mouth of the wound, from which later comes the form.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	 And it is necessary that when you see this instrument being prepared, that you first insert the probe to know the depth of the wound, so that what enters from the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and that it does not harm the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	 And if the instrument is larger, then it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with cloths, so that the instrument does not cause harm.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	 And it is necessary that he places the tip of the instrument above, and that he dips the instrument in.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	 And when the abscess opens, and one makes an opening with a soft hand, then it should be covered at the top, with warm butter.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	 And when the abscess is emptied, then you should put in the wound cloths soaked in rose oil or in dry green oil.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	 And put the cloth firmly at the bottom of the wound, and put another cloth on top of the wound and on the finger a clean cloth soaked in water where mallows have been cooked.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then the treatment afterwards for two days of dressing until it is healed.
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	 And sometimes lift the skin and the wound with a enema of water and honey, and then with water and lily roots and long Aristolochia cooked
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	 Then return to dressing.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	 And if the wound is festering in the flesh, then you must be careful not to use fire, but treat it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	 of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	 It is necessary first for the midwife to know the figure of natural childbirth, and the signs are when you see the woman push downwards and desire to smell air:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	 then the infant hastens to come out by force.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	 then know that this childbirth is according to natural figure, and the issue is under its head, and the second twin with it.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	 And when you see these signs, then you must gently press on the stomach, so that the child comes out quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	 because when it descends onto its head, then the afterbirth follows with it, and the mother is purged of her excesses by a good purging.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	 and this one that comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	 Because sometimes it comes feet first, and forcefully hits the body or head, or the hands, or comes onto its stomach, or back, and is turned by chance onto its neck, or into other evil shapes.
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	 therefore it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and skillful in these things, and to guard against error and deception, and I will show you all the positions how she should assist them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	 If the child comes out of its head by natural birth, and the woman gives birth violently, and the child's strength is weak, then have her sit on a saddle, where women hold her.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	 and let its nature be of oil or fenugreek, which should be cooked, and then have the woman drink between her teeth the small spatula of this form:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	 and cut open the afterbirth, and scrape at its nail until the moisture that is within flows out.
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	 and press the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then it is necessary to administer an enema to the woman with a mixture of fenugreek and castor oil.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	 then have her drink and cough with condiments, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour.
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	 If one now extracts the child.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	 And if both hands come out forcefully, then you must reset them lightly a little at a time.
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	 and if they cannot go back in, then place the woman on a seat, and lift her feet up high.
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	 then take the seat to the ground, and hold the woman so that she does not fall when standing up.
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	 and if the hand cannot go back in, and the child dies, then cut off the hands with the knife that was placed before, and extract the child, and reset them equally.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	 of the child's issue on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	 When the child comes out on its feet, then you must push it upwards;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	 and then turn it little by little until it is even.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	 Then take of garlic from the feet and stretch a little at a time.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	 When it reaches the thighs, command to take it and make him sneeze from it;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	 if it goes further, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	 And if he does not jump further as we have said, then turn him little by little until he is according to the natural figure.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	 For then he goes easily.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	 And if it does not go further as we have said, then take mustard seed from alder tree, and oil of sesame, and melted resin, and grind all in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	 and apply this mixture on the woman’s genital area both inside and outside of this application, then make her sit in hot water up to below the ribs.
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	 And when she is soaked underneath, give her a potion of honey, and place it underneath her, and leave it for an hour.
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	 then have her sit on the seat, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and gently press on her belly, for now the child jumps.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	 Of the child's birth on its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	 When the child comes in this manner, then put the midwife's hands there little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	 and let her be supported on her neck, and let her feet hang down, and let her lie on the bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	 and bend her hands little by little, and then press the hands on the belly, and remove the cushions from below, until she is prepared to come out.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	 and if the child does not jump, then take her feet and move them strongly, then move the belly upwards, then put your hands there.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	 And breastfeed the child a little at a time;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	 And command the woman to take hold of herself until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	 Of the child's birth who comes sideways with one hand hanging
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	 It is necessary to engineer the return of the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	 If it cannot be brought back, then make the woman rise and walk;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	 If she cannot walk, then make her lie on a bed, and spread her legs widely;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	 Then bring the midwife that I have mentioned;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	 And if she does not deliver, then make her sit on a chair, then study to return the hand.
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	 And breastfeed the child according to its natural position, and make it sneeze, and command her to take hold of herself until the child comes out forcefully.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	 from the child issuing on its neck, with hands spread and face turned towards the mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	 It is necessary that the patient hold his hand, then turn it little by little, and wash it gently.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	 And when it is healed, place on top the natural mucilage of althea and oil, as we have said, then instruct her to move it little by little.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	 And when you have done this, make her sit on a seat, and instruct her to take hold of herself.
et la fai esternuer.	 And make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	 of this same manner to all the second
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	 When it comes out in this manner to all the mucus, cut the mucus with your nail until the moisture is emptied.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	 And if the child comes up to his face and neck, cut it from the bottom so that it is not held back, and let the child die.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	 Then put the child inside, until you have placed him as is necessary, and instruct the woman to take hold of herself.
adonques si istra legierement.	 Then draw it out gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	 of the birth of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	 Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes three or four;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	 And this is not an unusual thing, and it happens rarely.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	 Two are an extraordinary thing, and they do not live, except for a few;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	 I know that if there are many, they are separated by the placenta which divides them, and it is attached to the womb.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	 And sometimes they come out just as naturally as a single one, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	 And if they come out violently, then care for them as we have said, and let the midwife be skilled, and do quickly and gently what she does.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	 And make sure to do so for health.
de plusors enfans	 of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	 Sometimes they are formed in the womb, one or two or three or four or five or six or seven, or more up to fifteen, and all are perfectly formed like a child by the measurement of the wise glorious one. And it is necessary that the doctor knows all this, because perhaps similar things happen to him;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	 Do so accordingly as needed.
de l’enfant mort	 of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	 When you treat a woman for a dead child or miscarriage, as I have said in the chapter on division, and it does not come out, and you are forced to work with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	 then you must know if the woman is of sound constitution and does not have any accidents or fear of death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	 If necessary, let the woman be placed on her back, with her head inclined downwards, and her legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	 And let the attendant place the cloth in two parts, so that she is tied to the bed and not moved during the birth of the child.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	 Then anoint the mouth of the woman in labor with moist oil, with a mixture of thyme and fenugreek and flaxseed, then let her wash her hands with these oils and mixtures.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	 Then gently pour them into the woman in labor, then seek a place where she can put the ointments conveniently, and beware if the child is ready to descend onto her head.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	 If she puts the ointments in her eyes or neck or mouth or under her tongue or chin or at the navel or near the ribs, and if the delivery is breech, then put them on the anus and in the lower ribs.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	 and it is necessary that he take the probe in his right hand, and place the tip between the fingers of the left hand, and thrust with all his hand gently, and insert the probe into one of these places that we have mentioned, until it reaches the empty space.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	 and this is the shape of the probe:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	 then insert against another probe, or the third if you need it, so that the extraction is equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	 and then they are equally tensed by moving from one side to the other, so that it comes out easily, and let the probes be notched for better grip, as shown in this shape:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	 And if part of it remains, then anoint the tip of one of his fingers with oil, and insert it into that part, and draw out the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	 And if there remains not a single one, then place this ointment in a higher place, and do so until it all comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	 And if one hand comes before the other and cannot be returned due to tightness, then you must wrap it in a cloth until it all comes out.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	 Then cut the nail at the base of the toe or with scissors, and so must you do for the other hand and the two feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	 And if the child's head is large and it is narrow at the exit, or has sharp pimples gathered on top, then you must insert the sharp tip of a stick between your fingers, pierce the top, and extract the liquid.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	 you will use the instrument called "almidach," from which the form comes with the instruments in the following chapter.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	 and do the same if the child has a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	 then draw out the bones with tongs, and if the head jumps out and is held by the forceps, it should be cut open until the moisture that is in the worst part comes out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	 and if it cannot come out, then chop it into pieces as you can;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	 and if he is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you must pierce him until the moisture flows out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	 And if the child is on its feet, then the traction is light, and the adjustment at the mouth of the womb is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	 And if he is swollen in the belly or the bladder, then you must extract it with a cloth wrapped around your hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	 And make a cut in the belly or the breast, until the moisture within is removed.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	 And if other members are taken away and the head remains, then the bailiff should put his hand into the marrow, and draw it out to the mouth of the marrow.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	 Then he puts in one or two more, and draws them strongly;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	 And if the mouth of the marrow is constricted by the hot abscess that has formed there, then it should not be probed, but rather moist and fatty things should be applied.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	 And the healer applies plasters and sieves in softening and moistening water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	 And if the child is out of its position, and you can put it back in place, then treat it as we have said for a living child.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	 And if one does not have power to remove it whole, then draw it out piece by piece, and leave nothing of the arrowhead.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	 And when you have done this, if the arrow comes into one of those abscesses that come in the flesh;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	 and if blood flows out, put it in boiling water to stop the bleeding, and apply other treatments to the arrow.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	 And I saw a woman in whose womb one child had died, then another was born on top of it, and the other also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	 After a long time, an abscess came to her womb, and it swelled so much that it burst, and she began to have great stench.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	 I was called to the care, and there I thought for a long time, but the wound could not be healed.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	 I placed a strong attracting plaster on it, and from it came out a bone, and after some days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	 I was greatly amazed by this, for the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	 Then I thought that it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	 I explored the wound, and drew out many bones until the woman was in a better state;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	 and the woman lived for a long time thus, and only occasionally did a little pus come out from the place.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	 and I have included this chapter only because when the master finds something strange, he should know how to help with it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	 To return the dislocation to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	 Here comes the form of the press, to which one turns the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	 and with two windings as two heads of two ropes.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	 Nevertheless, the horns should be more subtle than the restrictor, and should be made of ivory or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	 and the opening of the wood should be two fingers wide, and the margin of the trees one finger, and in length a palm and a half;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	 and between the two ropes should be two adjustments of this same wood, which are fastened on one and the other, half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	 and these two adjustments are pushed into the opening of the margin to open when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	 A different form, more subtle and lighter, should be made of ebony or boxwood, according to the appearance of tongs.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	 And it should have two heads and two adjustments, as you see, one palm long and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	 And when you see the instrument open completely, make the woman sit on the bed with her feet hanging and legs spread, then place the two adjustments together in the vagina, and hold the head of the instrument underneath between her thighs.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	 Then work your hand on the entire instrument, just as you did with the tongs, according to the amount that you see open the mouth of the vagina, until the cavity does what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	 This tool is all-encompassing, and its likenesses are many.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	 And when the surgeon has prepared them, then the work is more swift, and greater for men due to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	 Do not destroy the instrument before you have prepared it, because its needs are not negligible.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	 When the placenta is retained after childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, then make her sneeze forcefully, and hold your hands over her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	 And if she jumps because of this, it is good.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	 If not, then take a pot and make a hole in the lid, and put in herbs that can open the mother's mouth, such as hartwort, rue, anise, chamomile, cascara, and southernwood.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	 All these herbs, or some of them, are cooked in water on the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	 Then place a reed or hole in the pot, and the other end in the patient's mouth, and hold it until the steam enters the patient's mouth;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	 then make them sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	 Si il saute rapidement la deuxième fois.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	 And if she remains after this treatment and is not cured, then instruct the patient to moisten her left hand in mustard oil or althaea mucilage, and then insert it into the vagina, and seek a midwife.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	 and when she has found one, then take hold of it and pull it out little by little straight away, so that the patient does not twist during the extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	 But it must be moved gently to the right and left, then pull.
si venra et se desaerdra.	 It will come out and dislocate.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	 And if the mouth of the womb is narrowly constricted, we have said the treatment is sneezing and fumigating with herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	 And if it does not come out from all that we have said, take care not to be foolish in pulling.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	 But it is necessary that what is at the mouth of the womb, you tie to the thigh of the woman, then give her an enema with four-substance ointment.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	 Then she will fart and return it, and it will come out forcefully.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	 But nevertheless, when she farts, it causes a bad smell in the stomach and head, and injures the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	 Si therefore, it is necessary for appropriate fumigations to this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	 any of the ancients have proven fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	 The shape of the instrument used to fumigate the woman for retaining the flowers and the afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	 And it should be like a sieve, with the fine part facing the patient and the wide parts over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	 and let the fumigation be on the coals, and continue until the mange is destroyed, and then begin again with a new one.
de percier lou fondement	 To pierce the anus
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	 Many children are born whose anus is not open, but rather is obstructed by a fine membrane:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	 therefore it is necessary for the midwife to pierce that membrane with her finger, and not with an acute probe, and take care that she does not touch the intestine with it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then place a wet cloth soaked in wine and oil, then treat with unguent until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	 And if you doubt that it will not heal properly, place a lead plug in the hole, and leave it for several days, and have it removed when the child wants to go to bed.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	 And sometimes this obstruction comes from the sudden healing of a wound or abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	 then it is necessary to cover that sudden occurrence:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	 if it is treated, as we have said about the resin of fir.
de la fistule dou fondement	 of the fistula of the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	 Fistulas that come under the anus are nodular and swollen, which come near the anus or in the space of the two parts, if one has a fistula or several;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	 and when that nodulation is old, it works, and in addition, moisture produces white or subtle pus, and sometimes these fistulas are persistent;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	 And they are known by this: that there is vomiting or flatulence when the patient vomits, and sometimes it may be a stone.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	 And if there are fistulas that penetrate to the bladder, and halfway down the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	 and they reach as far as the hip joint, and even to the testicle.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	 And thus one knows the fistula penetrating the anus, and not penetrating:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	 and it is that you insert your index finger into the anus, and insert a thin needle of iron or steel into the fistula when there is no tortuosity.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	 And if there is tortuosity, then insert a thin tent of lead, or a horsehair, until you feel the tent or hair with your finger.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	 And if you do not feel it, and there is no excretion of feces or flatulence or bile, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	 know that it does not break through;
si te haste dou curer.	 if you hurry to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	 And when the fistula extends to the bladder or to the passage of the urine, then the urine leaks out and cannot be healed by medications.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	 If it breaks through to the hip joint, then the tendon comes to its place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	 if there is twisting and the sensation of pain around it, then it will always protrude, and neither medicine nor suturing by sewing helps;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	 and in these Persian fistulas there is no cure except hard work, and the foolishness of the doctors who meddle with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	 In those that are not Persian and not old, there is hope of health by iron, as I have proven, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on his back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	 And let him raise his legs up to his hips, and have his hips inclined towards his belly.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	 then put an iron tent, or of lead if there is torment, so that you know where the tent comes.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	 If the patient feels it around the anus, then you must put your index finger there, if you feel that the tent has pierced through;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	 and is revealed where you feel between your finger the pus or flesh, then know that it is perforated.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	 if one does not travel there, for it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	 One says however that some can be well healed, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	 and the aid that one does there is that one heats the subtle cautery according to the width of the fistula, as has been said before.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	 And he pours all hot into the fistula, until it reaches near the anus;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	 And do this two or three times, so that you know these hairs are burned, which resemble a bird feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	 And then treat it with moist compresses of butter, so that this hair comes out, then treat it with a greasy ointment and seal it.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	 If he is thus healed, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	 If so, it cannot be healed in any other way;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	 And if the tent enters and does not pierce through to the finger that is in the anus, and there is a thick covering of hair or silk between your finger and the tent, and you see the fistula at the place where the covering ends;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	 if at the beginning of the fistula, and always push the tent forward, and then after the cautery, until it reaches the end of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	 and the tent will be released, and it will fall;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	 then remove those charred parts that resemble a bird's feather, and nothing remains.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	 And if the blood flows, and passes between you and the work, then cauterize it with fire or with astringent medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	 Because the fire cautery combines two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	 that is to say, the burning of those charred parts, and the arresting of blood and drying out of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	 then treat wet tents with butter or powdered substance, until the place swells up, and the charred parts come out of the swelling;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	 Then heal the wound with immediate, quick-acting remedies that harden the flesh, and these remedies are dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	 Car when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	 And if the fistula reaches completely to the anus and is separated from the body, then push your finger into the anus and seek for it there.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	 If you feel the tent (and between II is the fabric or silk or cloth), where it is close to piercing, there should be no holes except for a path of faith and hope, through the administration of one of the III ways:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	 Or you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut to the bottom, or if you can, put tents there and treat as before;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	 And do not go too deep, lest you cut the tissue that holds the foundation, and uncontrolled bleeding occurs.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	 Then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	 By chance, it will be healed, or you remove that covering and clean it after it is cut near the foundation, either by tent or by another suitable instrument.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	 then cleanse that foul flesh which is in the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	 then strive to restore the wound and to close the fistula in the part below the foundation.
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	 this would be less painful for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	 And sometimes there are fistulas according to this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	 and when you insert the tent into the fistula, and it is on the side of the foundation near the skin above, then take a tent pierced at the tip in this manner:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	 And put a twisted thread in it, and push the tent along with all the thread into the fistula until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	 If it is going through the edge of the foundation inside, then draw out the thread of that hole, so that you insert your finger into the foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	 And pull the head of the thread, and gather the two heads together, and press them against each other, and leave it for one day or two.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	 And restrain it several times, until the thread cuts these sutures that are between them, and fall out;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	 then heal the wound until it is healed and cured.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	 If the fistula does not break through, have it pierced in every way that you can, unless it is too deeply embedded.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Because it is not appropriate to cover the wound for the binding if it is too deep, and then treat it, as we have said, until it heals.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	 The form of the thorny cautery with which one makes the fistula is very sharp on one side and cutting;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	 and on the other side not, so that one does not cut that which should not be cut, as you see here.
des emorroydes	 hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	 There are two kinds of emorydes:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	 either they are inside the anus, like seeds of pine, and there may be small or large ones, and blood always flows from them, and there may be one or several, and they protrude outside the anus and at the opening of the anus.
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	 But those which are without have little moisture, yet still sometimes a little green water or a little blood, and they have the color of the body.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	 And the treatment for those who have them inside the anus is such that you instruct the patient to strain himself to go into rooms until the anus excretes them, and the threads appear.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	 If you are quick, then seize it with tweezers or hold it with your nail, then cut it at its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	 And if the tweezers cannot hold them because of their moisture, then take them with a small cloth or cotton, or a piece of camlet.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	 And pull them with your fingers, then cut them, and sprinkle some hot powders that are available for cautery on top.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	 or you cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then continue with other treatments until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	 and if the fundament cannot pass, then give the patient an enema with harsh and bitter clyster to cleanse what is in the fundament, so that it may pass freely;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	 when the patient takes it, and if the feces are hard near the fundament, then the treatment is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	 and it is that you take them with your nail or with tweezers, and cut them, then treat as we have said, until they are healed, and that they avoid cutting with iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	 So you must apply the treatment in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	 Pull I thread twisted, and put it in a needle, then draw the thread above and make the needle pierce from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, and let it be wide.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	 And hold the thread firmly, then tie the thread, and pull out the needle, and do this with all the others, and leave one for draining the excess blood.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	 Then place a wet cloth soaked in rose oil or wax on the wound, and place it on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then leave it until it heals, and when it has healed, treat it with ointment and other treatments, until it is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	 Of dryness of the intestines or rectum
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	 Many times there is dryness in the intestines due to natural constraint and when the illness is old and medicine is of no use.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	 If you must, use the tip of a spatula or your nail to scrape off the scab on top, so that it does not become wet.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	 then cure it until it is dried as required;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	 and if it cannot dry, then renew the scraping more strongly than before, until it bleeds profusely and is scraped clean;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then cure it until it is healed.
dou fremit	 Of trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	 An insect is a small creature found under the skin, and goes very deep into it;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	 sometimes the cold finds it, and one feels it as if frozen to death with shivering, and this happens throughout the body, and more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	 And the treatment is such that you take a quill from a goose feather, or a strong ox feather, and place this quill on the shivering, so that the circle of redness surrounds the shivering entirely;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	 Then turn your hand along the whole chain until you cut all around the trembling, and put it in completely, and pull out the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	 And if you see it this way, then do so with a cane of brass or iron in this form, and let it be sharp below and drawn above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	 Do not pierce, to hold it at two, and press it together.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	 And if you see it, then cauterize the trembling as described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	 of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	 Sometimes a clyster is made of silver or gold, or melted bronze or iron.
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	 And sometimes these instruments are made in small and large sizes, according to those for whom they are intended.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	 Therefore, those [instruments] that are prepared for the treatment of children who are weak and in pain are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	 The shape of the small and large enema is thus wide at the top, where the stomach is tied like this:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	 And if there is a rupture where the stomach is tied as you see, and the head is pierced inside;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	 And let there be on one side two holes, and on the other one.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	 And let the bag where the medicines are placed be made of an animal's bladder or parchment, and let it be pierced all around with small holes, and let there be a finger's width between each hole. Then put into these holes a strong thread of twisted silk in the shape of an X or O, and gather the bag like a purse;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	 And when the medicines are inside, tie it to the instrument in front with a strong thread, then enema.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	 and this is the shape of a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	 And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the enema with oil or egg yolk, or something similar, then insert it lightly.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	 then the minister should press with both hands together until it is completely empty; then extract the enema, and have the patient raise their legs against the wall, and if the medicine wants to come out, hold it as long as possible;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	 And if he sleeps all night through, the aid is even greater.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if you enema him in illness of a prolapsed belly, and the medicine hastens to come out, then repeat it until he is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	 And if there are hemorrhoids in the anus or abscess, let the enema be as fine as for a child of one year.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	 and this is the form of the subtle enema which requires the skin to be tight:
des plaies	 of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	 We have already said in the section on wound treatment;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	 or we will tell you the treatments of hands and medicines, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	 I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made of, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and by what they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	 Les blessures peuvent être causées par la chute de pierres, ou par des coups d'épée et de couteau, ou de lance, ou de bâton, ou de flèche, ou par des choses similaires.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	 ou qui dépendent de la localisation dans le corps, comme une blessure sur le cou, ou sur la tête, ou sur les pieds, ou sur l'estomac, ou sur le foie, ainsi que d'autres parties similaires.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	 Et je vous expliquerai le traitement pour chaque blessure, et je commencerai par les blessures simples de la tête, car leur traitement sera rappelé dans ce chapitre.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	 Je dis que lorsqu'une simple blessure survient à la tête et que l'os n'est pas brisé, il faut faire attention si elle a été causée par la chute de pierres ou des choses similaires. Même si le cuir est rompu et que la blessure est grande, et que tu crains légèrement qu'un abcès se forme :
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	 if he does so immediately bleed from the head itself, even if a little blood comes from the wound, and let the bleeding be opposite to the injured part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	 and have the patient avoid overeating wine and heavy foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	 And if he does not want to bleed, let his food be reduced, and he should drink no wine, nor eat any meat;
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	 and place on the wound, if an abscess appears there, cotton soaked in rose oil alone, or in stiffened wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	 and if there is no hot abscess, then place on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood, and it has not been moved by the air, powder, which I will mention a little later;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if the fire has moved it, apply some ointments until he is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	 Et si la plaie est grande comme celle d'une tailleuse d'épée et semblable, et les lèvres ne peuvent pas se réunir par tentes, alors réunissez-les par couture, comme je le dirai pour les plaies du ventre, de la couture.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	 If the wound is exposed to the bone, and hollowed out, and holds only by a little, then cut it off;
