par aventure feroit venir la mort.	 perhaps it would bring death.
des dislocations de la hainche	 of hip dislocations
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	 Know that in the joints of the hip and in the joints of the shoulder, only dislocation occurs, and not as in other joints;
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	 And the hip joint is dislocated in four parts.
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	 within and without, and before and behind
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	 and more within than elsewhere, and rarely dislocated in front or back.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	 And the sign of its dislocation within is that when one joins the sick leg with the healthy one, it is longer, and the patient's knee opens more than the healthy one, and the patient cannot bend his knee as much.
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	 And it is the place which is near an abscess that is hot, because the head of the thigh comes there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	 And the sign of those to whom it happens as a result is that this event is contrary to the previous ones.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	 And the sign of the one to whom it happens in front, is that he stretches his leg according to the accomplishment;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	 nevertheless, he does not bend his knee without pain, and if one wants to make him walk, he cannot go forward, and holds his urine, and swells the ankle, and when he walks, he steps on the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	 And the sign of those to whom it happens afterwards is that they cannot extend their knee or bend it, and that leg is more twisted than the other, and the ankle is softened, and the head of the thigh is in the place below the hips.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	 The remedy for this kind of dislocation is that you return it if the dislocation is old, and it remains according to its condition, then there is no treatment; ‌
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	 and he should not have any presumption about it.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	 And in that which is the recent dislocation, and this is of the four types of dislocation, so hasten that you turn the joint, and push it inward and outward, and move it to the right and left;
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	 perhaps it will return [to its original place], and no other treatment is necessary.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	 And if it does not return in this manner, then you must prepare a strong support, and hold the leg strongly with two hands, or one strap that is tied above the knee;
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	 and another assistant should extend his hand on top in such a manner that he places his hands underneath the soles, then pulls with a soft strap around the thigh;
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	 and another holds the end of the strap;
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	 and they extend upwards and downwards all at once, so that the patient is lifted off the ground all at once, and remains hanging.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	 This manner of extension is common to four similar things, and if the dislocation returns, as we have said, it is well.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	 If not, then one must apply care to its likeness.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	 When the dislocation is in the hip, it is necessary that you place the patient on his healthy side, then put the ligament on the root of the thigh, and the place that is below the ankle, then extend the ligament upwards towards the ankle and towards the shin.
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	 Then take other assistants his arms, and embrace the thick part of the sick thigh, and extend it strongly with force.
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	 then it will return to its place now.
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	 And this method of dislocation is lighter than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	 And if you cannot set it in the manner we have said, then you must bind the two feet of the patient together with a strong, soft ligature above the two ankles, and above the two knees, and let the diseased leg be stretched two fingers' width more than the other.
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	 then let them hang from a pole over the head, and let them be about two arms' length above the ground.
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	 then command one attendant to grasp the thigh above the joint, and let another attendant hang with the patient, who grasps the thigh firmly, for the joint will now return quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	 And when the dislocation is over, let the patient lie down as we have said for one who has paralysis, and tighten the ligature properly around the diseased leg, and also around the foot.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	 Then put two tapers, one at the head and another at the feet, then insert a taper between the thighs of the patient in this manner;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	 And let it be surrounded by moistened cloths so that the patient is not burned, then let each assistant approach him, and the doctor align the dislocation with his hand.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	 If it returns, that is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	 If not, lay him on the table and press as we have said in the dislocation, and let the patient lie on his healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	 And when the dislocation is forward, then it is necessary to straighten the injured leg quickly, as I have said.
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	 And let the doctor place his weight on the injured ankle, then press with the other hand and straighten down towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	 And if the dislocation is backward, then it should not be straightened downward or lifted from the ground, but rather the patient should be positioned as if the hip were dislocated backward, as we have said about lying on two hips.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	 And let it be on its face, and the ligaments extended as we have said before, and one should press on the joint at the table.
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	 And it will be ready when the patient extends his legs, and they are equal.
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	 Then join the thighs, and place a poultice, and restrain with a bandage, so that the hip does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	 And rest for three days or four, then dislocate it again, and place the poultice on top.
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	 And if you see that they are equal, then restrain as before, and leave for three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 Then dislocate it again, and have the patient walk comfortably until the limb is healed.
de la dislocation dou genoil	 Of knee dislocation
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	 The knee is dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	 that is to say, inward, outward, and backward.
et ne desalue point devant.	 and does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	 And the sign is that you instruct the patient to bend his leg at the thigh, and if it does not bend at the thigh, know that it is dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	 And the restoration of all (three types) is that you make the patient sit upright and extend his leg if he can, and place your back against his face, and put his foot on your feet.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	 Then take his knee in your palms, and pull it between your thighs, then bend the two sides of the knee strongly.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	 And another assistant extends his foot until the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that he can bend his leg at the thigh easily. xspace
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	 And place the plaster on it, and bind the leg to the thigh, and keep them together strongly for three days or four, then unbind it.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 And let the patient not try to walk until the limb is healed.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	 And if the limb is not perfectly straight, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	 of the ankle dislocation
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	 The ankles are sometimes moved and sometimes fully dislocated, inside and out.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	 And the sign is that the ankle is swollen and protrudes towards the dislocated part.
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	 The reduction should be gentle, and it should be stretched gently with his hands when only slightly moved.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	 And when it is completely dislocated, you must have the patient sit upright, and have one helper hold on to the leg above the ankle.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	 Then pull the foot towards you with your right hand, and then with the left two times, then stretch it upwards, and push the foot upwards nicely.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	 And do this two times, as we have said, by pushing and pulling the foot.
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	 if it returns, that is good;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	 but if not, then begin the work again, for it will return;
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	 and if it cannot return thus, then make the patient lie on their back on the ground, and drive a stake firmly into the ground between their thighs, and tie cloths around it, so that it does not wound the patient.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	 then let one of the assistants hold the thigh, and another assistant extend the foot with his hands or with a strap that he ties above the ankle.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	 then let each assistant extend equally, and the stake should always be between the patient's thighs to hold the patient when stretching.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	 Then let the doctor reset the dislocation with his hands, and another assistant hold the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	 And when it is well set, then place the bandage and cloths on top, and bind tightly, and tie the foot to the leg, and watch out for the nerves that are behind the ankle, so that the ligature is not too tight;
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	 then leave it for two or three days, and if the bandage loosens, bind again;
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	 then unbind on the third or fourth day, and prevent the patient from walking for four days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	 and if he walks before this time, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if a boil comes here, you must soothe it, as we have said elsewhere, until it is healed.
des dois	 two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	 When the fingers are dislocated, they must be gently stretched without strain, and this is a light task.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	 Et si la dislocation est dans une articulation du dos ou du pied, il faut que tu fasses asseoir le malade sur une surface plane ou sur une table droite, et mets ton pied sur ce qui dépasse de ces articulations, puis presse fortement avec ton pied jusqu'à ce qu'il revienne à sa place.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	 Et quand il est de nouveau aligné et que rien ne dépasse, alors place sous la plante du pied une planche avec deux chevilles. Ensuite, serre fortement et laisse reposer pendant trois jours, puis desserre.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Et fais-le reposer jusqu'à ce qu'il soit guéri.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	 Of wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	 Lorsqu'une blessure accompagne la dislocation et que l'on veut la réparer, il arrive souvent que le patient meurt.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	 If you are not skilled in the art and have not practiced it for a long time, do not be presumptuous in the cure; and if you are not compassionate, merciful, and patient, do not be bold;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	 Use at first things that calm a hot abscess, and leave the patient in God's hands if you do not see hope for health;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	 And when you see hope, then reset the limb in place immediately, before the hot abscess comes.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	 And when the limb is in place, administer things that calm a hot abscess, and treat the wound as needed with dried onions.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	 And if there is also a fracture with the dislocation and small bones are displaced, remove them and do as we have said for simple diseases.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	 And beware of entering into a state of fear, as I have said, for it is worthless according to your Creator, and for the skill of your weapon and your body.
